"DOTA_Patch_7_11_General_6"	"Die AoE-Goldprämie für das zurückliegende Team skaliert nicht länger basierend auf der Differenz der Teamgesamtvermögens, sondern nur noch auf dem individuellen Vermögen des fallenden Helden. Bisher führte ein einzelner gut verdienender Held in Ihrem Team dazu, dass die Gegner sehr viel mehr Gold erhielten, auch wenn sie nur einen Unterstützerhelden Ihres Teams töteten."
"[english]DOTA_Patch_7_11_General_6"	"AoE gold for the losing team no longer scales with the overall team networth difference, just the individual networth of the dying hero. Previously, a core on your team doing really well meant that a support on your team dying gave an increasing amount of gold to the enemy."

It now has 5 rounds, each round Radiant and Dire pick 1 hero each at the same time and the selections each team makes is hidden until the next round. "[english]DOTA_Patch_7_25_General_2"	"Reworked how hero banning works in All Pick. Previously half of the voted heroes would get banned. Now each ban has a 50% chance of succeeding. If there are less than 10 heroes banned, heroes will automatically roll for banning based on their ban rate at your MMR bracket."
